<anml version="1.0"  xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
	<automata-network id="automata">
		<state-transition-element id="0" symbol-set="[\x4a]" start="all-input">
			<report-on-match reportcode="0"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="1" symbol-set="[\x52]" start="all-input">
			<report-on-match reportcode="0"/>
		</state-transition-element>
	</automata-network>
</anml>
module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 74 || character == 82);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste0ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);


	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

<anml version="1.0"  xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
	<automata-network id="automata">
		<state-transition-element id="0" symbol-set="[\x52]" start="all-input">
			<activate-on-match element="1"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="1" symbol-set="[\x4f]">
			<activate-on-match element="2"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="2" symbol-set="[\x4d]">
			<activate-on-match element="3"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="3" symbol-set="[\x45]">
			<activate-on-match element="4"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="4" symbol-set="[\x4f]">
			<report-on-match reportcode="0"/>
		</state-transition-element>
	</automata-network>
</anml>
module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 82);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 79);
endmodule

module STE2(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 77);
endmodule

module STE3(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 69);
endmodule

module STE4(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 79);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active, ste2Active, ste3Active, ste4Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate, ste2ChildrenActivate, ste3ChildrenActivate, ste4ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
	STE2 ste2(character, ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
	STE3 ste3(character, ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
	STE4 ste4(character, ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);
	FF ste2FF(ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste2Active);
	FF ste3FF(ste2ChildrenActivate, clock, ste3Active);
	FF ste4FF(ste3ChildrenActivate, clock, ste4Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("2: %d %d", ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
			$display("3: %d %d", ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
			$display("4: %d %d", ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste4ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active, ste2Active, ste3Active, ste4Active, ste5Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate, ste2ChildrenActivate, ste3ChildrenActivate, ste4ChildrenActivate, ste5ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
	STE2 ste2(character, ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
	STE3 ste3(character, ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
	STE4 ste4(character, ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
	STE5 ste5(character, ste5Active, ste5ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);
	FF ste2FF(ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste2Active);
	FF ste3FF(ste2ChildrenActivate, clock, ste3Active);
	FF ste4FF(ste3ChildrenActivate, clock, ste4Active);
	FF ste5FF(ste4ChildrenActivate, clock, ste5Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("2: %d %d", ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
			$display("3: %d %d", ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
			$display("4: %d %d", ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
			$display("5: %d %d", ste5Active, ste5ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste5ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 74 || character == 82);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 79 || character == 85);
endmodule

module STE2(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && ((76 <= character && character <= 77));
endmodule

module STE3(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 69 || character == 73);
endmodule

module STE4(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 79);
endmodule

module STE5(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 69);
endmodule

module STE6(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 84);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active, ste2Active, ste3Active, ste4Active, ste5Active, ste6Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate, ste2ChildrenActivate, ste3ChildrenActivate, ste4ChildrenActivate, ste5ChildrenActivate, ste6ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
	STE2 ste2(character, ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
	STE3 ste3(character, ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
	STE4 ste4(character, ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
	STE5 ste5(character, ste5Active, ste5ChildrenActivate);
	STE6 ste6(character, ste6Active, ste6ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);
	FF ste2FF(ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste2Active);
	FF ste3FF(ste2ChildrenActivate, clock, ste3Active);
	FF ste4FF(ste3ChildrenActivate, clock, ste4Active);
	FF ste5FF(ste3ChildrenActivate, clock, ste5Active);
	FF ste6FF(ste5ChildrenActivate, clock, ste6Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("2: %d %d", ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
			$display("3: %d %d", ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
			$display("4: %d %d", ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
			$display("5: %d %d", ste5Active, ste5ChildrenActivate);
			$display("6: %d %d", ste6Active, ste6ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste4ChildrenActivate || ste6ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);

			$display("report: %d", ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active, ste2Active, ste3Active, ste4Active, ste5Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate, ste2ChildrenActivate, ste3ChildrenActivate, ste4ChildrenActivate, ste5ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
	STE2 ste2(character, ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
	STE3 ste3(character, ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
	STE4 ste4(character, ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
	STE5 ste5(character, ste5Active, ste5ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);
	FF ste2FF(ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste2Active);
	FF ste3FF(ste2ChildrenActivate, clock, ste3Active);
	FF ste4FF(ste3ChildrenActivate, clock, ste4Active);
	FF ste5FF(ste4ChildrenActivate, clock, ste5Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("2: %d %d", ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
			$display("3: %d %d", ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
			$display("4: %d %d", ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
			$display("5: %d %d", ste5Active, ste5ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste5ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 82);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 10 || character == 32 || (40 <= character && character <= 43) || (45 <= character && character <= 46) || character == 63 || (65 <= character && character <= 90) || character == 92 || (97 <= character && character <= 122) || character == 124);
endmodule

module STE2(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 10 || character == 32 || (40 <= character && character <= 43) || (45 <= character && character <= 46) || character == 63 || (65 <= character && character <= 90) || character == 92 || (97 <= character && character <= 122) || character == 124);
endmodule

module STE3(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 69);
endmodule

module STE4(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 79);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active, ste2Active, ste3Active, ste4Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate, ste2ChildrenActivate, ste3ChildrenActivate, ste4ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
	STE2 ste2(character, ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
	STE3 ste3(character, ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
	STE4 ste4(character, ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);
	FF ste2FF(ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste2Active);
	FF ste3FF(ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate || ste2ChildrenActivate, clock, ste3Active);
	FF ste4FF(ste3ChildrenActivate, clock, ste4Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);

		end
	end

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 82);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 10 || character == 32 || (40 <= character && character <= 43) || (45 <= character && character <= 46) || character == 63 || (65 <= character && character <= 90) || character == 92 || (97 <= character && character <= 122) || character == 124);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate || ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

	<automata-network id="automata">
		<state-transition-element id="0" symbol-set="[\x2b]" start="all-input">
			<report-on-match reportcode="0"/>
		</state-transition-element>
	</automata-network>
</anml>
module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 43);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste0ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);


	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

<anml version="1.0"  xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
	<automata-network id="automata">
		<state-transition-element id="0" symbol-set="[\x2e]" start="all-input">
			<activate-on-match element="1"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="1" symbol-set="[\x3f]">
			<activate-on-match element="2"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="2" symbol-set="[\x7c]">
			<activate-on-match element="3"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="3" symbol-set="[\x2b]">
			<activate-on-match element="4"/>
		</state-transition-element>
		<state-transition-element id="4" symbol-set="[\x2a]">
			<report-on-match reportcode="0"/>
		</state-transition-element>
	</automata-network>
</anml>
module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 46);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 63);
endmodule

module STE2(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 124);
endmodule

module STE3(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 43);
endmodule

module STE4(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 42);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active, ste2Active, ste3Active, ste4Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate, ste2ChildrenActivate, ste3ChildrenActivate, ste4ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
	STE2 ste2(character, ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
	STE3 ste3(character, ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
	STE4 ste4(character, ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);
	FF ste2FF(ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste2Active);
	FF ste3FF(ste2ChildrenActivate, clock, ste3Active);
	FF ste4FF(ste3ChildrenActivate, clock, ste4Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("2: %d %d", ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
			$display("3: %d %d", ste3Active, ste3ChildrenActivate);
			$display("4: %d %d", ste4Active, ste4ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste4ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 10 || character == 32 || (40 <= character && character <= 43) || (45 <= character && character <= 46) || (65 <= character && character <= 90) || character == 92 || (97 <= character && character <= 122) || character == 124);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 63);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1ChildrenActivate);


	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: S %d", ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 10 || character == 32 || (40 <= character && character <= 43) || (45 <= character && character <= 46) || character == 63 || (65 <= character && character <= 90) || character == 92 || (97 <= character && character <= 122) || character == 124);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 63);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate || ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule

module STE0(
	input [7:0] character,

);
	assign activateChildren = (character == 65);
endmodule

module STE1(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 67);
endmodule

module STE2(
	input [7:0] character,
	input isActive,
	output activateChildren
);
	assign activateChildren = isActive && (character == 84);
endmodule

module FF(
	input setActive,
	input clock,
	output reg isActive
);
	always @(posedge clock)
		isActive <= setActive;
endmodule

module main();
	integer fin, bytesRead;
	reg [7:0] character;
	reg clock;

	wire ste1Active, ste2Active;
	wire ste0ChildrenActivate, ste1ChildrenActivate, ste2ChildrenActivate;

	STE0 ste0(character, ste0ChildrenActivate);
	STE1 ste1(character, ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
	STE2 ste2(character, ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);

	FF ste1FF(ste0ChildrenActivate, clock, ste1Active);
	FF ste2FF(ste1ChildrenActivate, clock, ste2Active);

	always #5 clock = !clock;

	initial
	begin
		fin = $fopen("input.txt", "rb");
		clock = 0;

		while (1)
		begin
			bytesRead = $fread(character, fin, 0, 1);
			if (bytesRead < 1)
				$finish;

			#1;

			$display("Character: %h", character);
			$display("0: S %d", ste0ChildrenActivate);
			$display("1: %d %d", ste1Active, ste1ChildrenActivate);
			$display("2: %d %d", ste2Active, ste2ChildrenActivate);
			$display("report: %d", ste2ChildrenActivate);
			$display();

			#9;
		end
	end
endmodule
